focus = {
	id = SOV_Introduce_NEP
	text = RUS_Introduce_NEP
	icon = GFX_RUS_Introduce_NEP
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = { focus = SOV_Premier_Bukharin }
	relative_position_id = SOV_Premier_Bukharin
	x = 0
	y = 1
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = nsp_in_power
			has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_I_Bukharin_hog_rso
		}
	}
	bypass = { 
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_New_Economic_Policy_modifier }
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOV_Introduce_NEP"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = rus_unfinished_land_reform
			}
			destroy_unfinished_land_reform = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		country_event = rusdem.309
		set_variable = { RUS_NEP_global_building_slots_factor = 0.1 }
		set_variable = { RUS_NEP_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = -0.06 }
		set_variable = { RUS_NEP_production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor = 0.03 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nep_market = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nep_state = 3 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nep_worker = 1 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nep_peasant = 3 }
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_New_Economic_Policy_modifier }
	}
}

focus = {
	id = SOV_Smychka
	text = RUS_Smychka
	icon = GFX_RUS_Promote_Smychka
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = { focus = SOV_Introduce_NEP }
	relative_position_id = SOV_Premier_Bukharin
	x = -1
	y = 2
	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = nsp_in_power
			has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_I_Bukharin_hog_rso
		}
	}
	bypass = { 
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_bypass_nep
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 40 }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOV_Smychka"
		country_event = rusdem.312
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = RUS_upk }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { RUS_nep_worker > RUS_nep_peasant } }
			RUS_nep_increase_peasant = yes
		}
		else = {
			RUS_nep_increase_worker = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			RUS_NEP_stability_factor = 0.05 
			tooltip = stability_factor_tooltip
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			RUS_NEP_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = 0.03 
			tooltip = production_factory_max_efficiency_factor_tooltip
		}		
	}
}

			name = RUS_Centralized_Logistics 
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = train_tech
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 653 decision = RUS_Expand_Transsiberian_railways_EKB_OMSK }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 571 decision = RUS_Expand_Transsiberian_railways_OMSK_KRASNOYARSK }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 563 decision = RUS_Expand_Transsiberian_railways_KRASNOYARSK_CHITA }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 408 decision = RUS_Expand_Transsiberian_railways_CHITA_VLADI }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				is_subject = no
				country_exists = TRM
			}
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = RUS_expand_railways_teams }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 566 decision = RUS_supply_buff }
		}	
	}
}
